# âœ… What this does (fully automated)

- **Ops alert on every form submission**Â â†’ posts a clean summary to yourÂ **Discord #ops**.
    
- **Oneâ€‘click approvals**Â â†’ when you tickÂ **Approved**Â in the sheet, itÂ **autoâ€‘posts the invite**Â to yourÂ **Telegram channel**Â (and to Discord Broadcast if you want).

# ğŸ”§ Paste this WHOLE file intoÂ `Code.gs`

_(It uses the properties you already set:Â `DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK`,Â `DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK`,Â `TG_BOT_TOKEN`,Â `TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID`. Optional:Â `TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK`Â if you want the post to include the private invite link.)_

``/***** CONFIG-LESS: pulls secrets from Script Properties *****/ function _props() {   return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties(); }  /***** LOW-LEVEL SENDERS *****/ function _sendDiscord(webhook, content) {   if (!webhook) return;   UrlFetchApp.fetch(webhook, {     method: 'post',     contentType: 'application/json',     payload: JSON.stringify({ content }),     muteHttpExceptions: true   }); }  function _sendTelegram(token, chatId, text) {   if (!token || !chatId) return;   const url = 'https://api.telegram.org/bot' + token + '/sendMessage';   UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {     method: 'post',     contentType: 'application/json',     payload: JSON.stringify({ chat_id: chatId, text, parse_mode: 'HTML', disable_web_page_preview: true }),     muteHttpExceptions: true   }); }  /***** DUAL BRIDGE (TG + Discord Broadcast) *****/ function sendToBridge(message) {   const P = _props();   _sendTelegram(P.TG_BOT_TOKEN, P.TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID, message);   _sendDiscord(P.DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK, message); }  /***** RENDERING *****/ function renderHtml_(nv) {   // nv is e.namedValues: { "Question Title": ["value"] , ... }   let rows = '';   Object.keys(nv).forEach(k => {     const v = Array.isArray(nv[k]) ? nv[k].join(', ') : String(nv[k] || '');     rows += `<tr><td style="padding:4px 8px"><b>${escapeHtml_(k)}</b></td><td style="padding:4px 8px">${escapeHtml_(v)}</td></tr>`;   });   return (     `<b>ğŸ“ New Vetting Submission</b>\n` +     `<i>(auto-routed by VaultOps_Bridge)</i>\n\n` +     `<b>Compact:</b> ${escapeHtml_(compactLine_(nv))}\n\n` +     `<b>Details</b>\n` +     `<pre>${escapeHtml_(JSON.stringify(nv, null, 2))}</pre>`   ); }  // Short one-liner for #ops function renderOpsSummary_(nv) {   const alias = pick_(nv, ['Alias','Handle','Username','Name']);   const role  = pick_(nv, ['Role','Position','Category']);   const email = pick_(nv, ['Email','E-mail']);   const tg    = pick_(nv, ['Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle','Signal','TG','Telegram handle']);   return `ğŸ†• Vetting: ${alias || 'N/A'} Â· ${role || 'N/A'} Â· ${email || 'N/A'} Â· ${tg || 'N/A'}`; }  function compactLine_(nv) {   const alias = pick_(nv, ['Alias','Handle','Username','Name']);   const role  = pick_(nv, ['Role','Position','Category']);   const region= pick_(nv, ['Country','Region','City','Location']);   return `${alias || 'N/A'} Â· ${role || 'N/A'} Â· ${region || 'N/A'}`; }  function pick_(nv, keys) {   for (const k of keys) {     if (k in nv) {       const val = Array.isArray(nv[k]) ? nv[k][0] : nv[k];       if (val) return String(val);     }   }   return ''; }  function escapeHtml_(s) {   return String(s)     .replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;')     .replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/'/g,'&#39;'); }  /***** EVENTS *****/ // 1) OPS alert on every submission (From spreadsheet â†’ On form submit) function onFormSubmit(e) {   try {     const P = _props();     const ops = P.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK;     const nv  = e && e.namedValues ? e.namedValues : {};     // send compact to #ops     _sendDiscord(ops, renderOpsSummary_(nv));     // optional: also mirror full to broadcast? keep ops clean by default.     // sendToBridge(renderHtml_(nv));  // uncomment if you want full details broadcasted too   } catch (err) {     logErr('onFormSubmit', err);   } }  // 2) Approvals: when you tick the "Approved" checkbox, broadcast invite // (This runs automatically on any edit in the sheet) function onEdit(e) {   try {     const sheet = e.range.getSheet();     const editedCol = e.range.getColumn();     const editedRow = e.range.getRow();      // Find the "Approved" column by header text (row 1)     const headers = sheet.getRange(1,1,1,sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase() === 'approved') + 1;     if (!approvedCol) return;      // Only react if the Approved column changed to TRUE     if (editedCol !== approvedCol) return;     const val = sheet.getRange(editedRow, approvedCol).getValue();     if (val !== true) return;      // Build a short approval message from the row     const rowVals = sheet.getRange(editedRow, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const rowObj = {};     headers.forEach((h,i)=> rowObj[String(h)] = rowVals[i]);      const P = _props();     const invite = P.TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK ? `\n\nğŸ”— <a href="${P.TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK}">Private Invite Link</a>` : '';     const msg =       `âœ… <b>Approved:</b> ${escapeHtml_(compactLine_(rowObj))}${invite}`;      // Broadcast to TG + Discord broadcast     sendToBridge(msg);   } catch (err) {     logErr('onEdit', err);   } }  /***** UTIL *****/ function logErr(where, err) {   const P = _props();   const text = `âŒ ${where}: ${err && err.message ? err.message : err}\n` +                (err && err.stack ? `<pre>${escapeHtml_(err.stack)}</pre>` : '');   // try to surface to ops   _sendDiscord(P.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, text); }  /***** MANUAL TEST *****/ function testBridge() {   sendToBridge('ğŸš€ VaultOps Bridge test â€” Telegram + Discord are live.'); }``

# ğŸ”§ Add this config + helpers (top of Code.gs)

`/*** === AUTO-VET BASELINE (EDIT ME) === ***/ const RULES = {   requiredFields: ['Email', 'Alias / Handle', 'Role'],   emailAllowDomains: ['proton.me','protonmail.com','gmail.com'],   // keep broad for now   emailBlockDomains: ['mailinator.com','tempmail','10min'],   minAnswerChars: 8,                                              // short = sus   blocklistWords: ['scam','pump','xxx','porn','nft','casino'],    // add as you see patterns   requireHandles: ['Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle','Signal','TG'], // at least one must be present   countryAllow: [],   // e.g., ['Philippines','United States']  (empty = allow all)   countryBlock: [],   // e.g., ['Russia','Nigeria']   duplicateKeys: ['Email','Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle'],   // used to detect repeats   autoApproveIf: (row) => {     // Example: Role contains â€œEx-Patâ€ or â€œVeteranâ€ and email not from blocklist     const role = (row['Role']||'').toString().toLowerCase();     const email = (row['Email']||'').toString().toLowerCase();     return (role.includes('ex-pat') || role.includes('expat') || role.includes('veteran')) &&            !/mailinator|tempmail|10min/.test(email);   },   autoRejectIf: (row) => {     // Example: any blocklist word in free-text answers     const txt = Object.values(row).join(' ').toLowerCase();     return RULES.blocklistWords.some(w => txt.includes(w));   } };  /*** === UTILS === ***/ function headerMap_(sheet){   const headers = sheet.getRange(1,1,1,sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const map = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> map[String(h).trim()] = i+1);   return {headers, map}; } function rowObject_(sheet, rowIndex){   const {headers,map} = headerMap_(sheet);   const vals = sheet.getRange(rowIndex,1,1,headers.length).getValues()[0];   const obj = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> obj[String(h)] = vals[i]);   return {obj, headers, map}; } function domainOf_(email){ const m = String(email||'').toLowerCase().match(/@([^>\s]+)/); return m?m[1]:''; }`

---

# ğŸ§  Auto-vet engine

``function decide_(row){   const reasons = [];   const r = RULES;    // Required fields   for (const key of r.requiredFields){     const v = (row[key]||'').toString().trim();     if (!v) reasons.push(`Missing required: ${key}`);   }    // At least one handle   const hasAnyHandle = r.requireHandles.some(k => String(row[k]||'').trim());   if (!hasAnyHandle) reasons.push('No Telegram/Signal handle');    // Email checks   const email = (row['Email']||'').toString().trim();   const dom = domainOf_(email);   if (dom){     if (r.emailBlockDomains.some(d => dom.includes(d))) reasons.push(`Blocked email domain: ${dom}`);     if (r.emailAllowDomains.length && !r.emailAllowDomains.some(d => dom.endsWith(d))){       reasons.push(`Unapproved email domain: ${dom}`);     }   } else {     reasons.push('Invalid/missing email');   }    // Country allow/block (if you use a Country column)   const country = (row['Country']||row['Location']||'').toString();   if (r.countryBlock.length && r.countryBlock.includes(country)) reasons.push(`Blocked country: ${country}`);   if (r.countryAllow.length && country && !r.countryAllow.includes(country)) reasons.push(`Not in allowlist country: ${country}`);    // Minimal length sanity (catches â€œokâ€, â€œ.â€ spam)   const shortAnswers = Object.values(row).filter(v => String(v||'').trim().length < r.minAnswerChars).length;   if (shortAnswers > 3) reasons.push('Many very short answers');    // Hard rules   if (r.autoRejectIf(row)) reasons.push('Matched auto-reject rule');    // Decision   if (!reasons.length && r.autoApproveIf(row)) {     return {decision:'APPROVE', score: 100, reasons:['Matched auto-approve rule']};   }   if (!reasons.length) {     return {decision:'REVIEW', score: 70, reasons:['Clean but needs human eyes']};   }   // If only â€œlightâ€ reasons (e.g., unknown domain) you can still route to REVIEW   const fatal = reasons.some(x => /blocked|invalid|missing required|auto-reject/i.test(x));   return {decision: fatal ? 'REJECT' : 'REVIEW', score: fatal ? 0 : 50, reasons}; }``

# ğŸ”— Wire it into your sheet events

### 1) Auto-vet on submit â†’ ping #ops + set Status, optionally auto-approve

``function onFormSubmit(e){   try{     const P = _props();  // from earlier file     const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();     const lastRow = ss.getLastRow();     const {obj, headers, map} = rowObject_(ss, lastRow);      // Ensure Status & Approved columns exist     if (!map['Status']) { ss.getRange(1, headers.length+1).setValue('Status'); map['Status']=headers.length+1; }     if (!map['Approved']) { ss.getRange(1, headers.length+2).setValue('Approved'); map['Approved']=headers.length+2;        ss.getRange(2, map['Approved'], ss.getMaxRows()-1, 1).insertCheckboxes(); }      // Decide     const res = decide_(obj);     ss.getRange(lastRow, map['Status']).setValue(res.decision + (res.reasons.length? (' â€” '+res.reasons.join('; ')) : '') );      // Auto-approve path     if (res.decision === 'APPROVE') {       ss.getRange(lastRow, map['Approved']).setValue(true); // triggers onEdit â†’ broadcast invite     }      // Ops ping summary     const summary = `ğŸ†• Vetting: ${compactLine_(obj)}\nDecision: ${res.decision}\nReasons: ${res.reasons.join(' | ') || 'â€”'}`;     _sendDiscord(P.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, summary);    }catch(err){ logErr('onFormSubmit', err); } }``

### 2) Approvals broadcast (you already have it)

Your existingÂ `onEdit(e)`Â will fire whenÂ **Approved = TRUE**Â and post the invite viaÂ `sendToBridge(msg)`.

# ğŸ“’ Audit trail (optional but smart)

Add this once to create/append an â€œAuditâ€ sheet so every decision is logged:

`function audit_(rowObj, decision, reasons){   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();   const sh = ss.getSheetByName('Audit') || ss.insertSheet('Audit');   if (sh.getLastRow() === 0) sh.appendRow(['Timestamp','Decision','Reasons','Compact','Raw JSON']);   sh.appendRow([new Date(), decision, reasons.join(' | '), compactLine_(rowObj), JSON.stringify(rowObj)]); }`

Then callÂ `audit_(obj, res.decision, res.reasons);`Â insideÂ `onFormSubmit`.

That error means you tried to apply theÂ **checkbox validation**Â directly on theÂ **header row (Row 1)**.

ğŸ‘‰ Data validation (checkboxes) only works on the rows beneath the header, not the header itself.

### Hereâ€™s how to fix it:

1. **Leave Row 1 alone**Â â€” just typeÂ `Approved`Â andÂ `Status`Â as plain text in Row 1 (your headers).

    `Timestamp | Name | Severity | Notes | Approved | Status`

    - So ifÂ `Approved`Â is column E, clickÂ **E2:E**Â (not E1).
        
    - Then go toÂ **Data â†’ Data validation**.
        
    - Set Criteria â†’Â **Checkbox**.
        
    - Save.
        
3. Now youâ€™ll see âœ… checkboxes in every row starting from row 2, while row 1 stays your header.

###### ChatGPT said:

Say less, Papi â€” hereâ€™s the exactÂ **row-monitor script**Â you need.  
When you tickÂ **Approved**Â on any row, it updatesÂ **Status**Â and blasts the message toÂ **Telegram + Discord**Â through yourÂ `sendToBridge()`.

### Paste this into yourÂ `Code.gs`Â (under your existing code)

``/**  * Fires automatically when you edit the sheet.  * If the edit flipped the "Approved" checkbox to TRUE,  * it updates Status and broadcasts via sendToBridge().  */ function onEdit(e) {   try {     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     // Optional: only react on the main form tab name (adjust if yours differs)     // if (sh.getName() !== 'Form Responses 1') return;      // Ignore header row edits     if (e.range.getRow() === 1) return;      // Find columns by header text in Row 1     const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const findCol = (name) =>       headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase() === name) + 1;      const approvedCol = findCol('approved');     const statusCol   = findCol('status');      if (!approvedCol) return;                     // no Approved column = nothing to do     if (e.range.getColumn() !== approvedCol) return; // not editing Approved col      const isApproved = e.range.getValue() === true;     const row = e.range.getRow();      // Pull the whole row as an object {Header: Value}     const values = sh.getRange(row, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const rowObj = {};     headers.forEach((h, i) => (rowObj[String(h)] = values[i]));      // Update Status text (create column if missing)     if (!statusCol) {       sh.getRange(1, headers.length + 1).setValue('Status');     }     const statusColumnIndex = statusCol || headers.length + 1;     sh.getRange(row, statusColumnIndex).setValue(isApproved ? 'Approved âœ…' : 'Unapproved â›”');      // Only broadcast when it becomes approved     if (!isApproved) return;      // Build a short message (edit as you like)     const alias = pickField_(rowObj, ['Alias', 'Alias / Handle', 'Handle', 'Username', 'Name']) || 'N/A';     const role  = pickField_(rowObj, ['Role', 'Position', 'Category']) || 'N/A';     const region= pickField_(rowObj, ['Country', 'Region', 'City', 'Location']) || 'N/A';      const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties();     const invite = props.TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK ? `\n\nğŸ”— <a href="${props.TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK}">Private Invite Link</a>` : '';      const msg =       `âœ… <b>Approved:</b> ${escapeHtml_(alias)} Â· ${escapeHtml_(role)} Â· ${escapeHtml_(region)}${invite}`;      // Blast to Telegram + Discord Broadcast     sendToBridge(msg);    } catch (err) {     logErr('onEdit', err); // uses your existing error helper   } }  /** helper to pick the first non-empty field from a list of header names */ function pickField_(obj, keys) {   for (const k of keys) {     if (k in obj && obj[k] !== '' && obj[k] != null) {       const v = Array.isArray(obj[k]) ? obj[k][0] : obj[k];       if (String(v).trim()) return String(v);     }   }   return ''; }``

### How to use it

1. Make sure you already have these headers in Row 1:Â **Approved**Â (with checkboxes in row 2 down) andÂ **Status**.
    
2. **No trigger needed**Â â€”Â `onEdit(e)`Â runs automatically.
    
3. TickÂ **Approved**Â on any row â†’
    
    - **Status**Â becomes â€œApproved âœ…â€
        
    - A message posts toÂ **Telegram**Â (your channel) +Â **Discord Broadcast**
        
    - If you setÂ `TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK`Â in Script Properties, itâ€™ll include theÂ **private invite link**.
        

### Optional polish

- If your form tab isnâ€™t â€œForm Responses 1â€, uncomment the tab check and set the exact name.
    
- Edit the 3 fields used in the message (`Alias`,Â `Role`,Â `Country/Region/City`) to match your exact headers.

Lockedâ€”this is theÂ **last piece**: a clean, conservativeÂ **auto-vet**Â that runs on each form submission, writesÂ **Status**, and (when clearly good)Â **ticks Approved**Â to fire your broadcast. Minimal knobs, safe defaults.

## What you paste (one block)

Drop thisÂ **above**Â your existingÂ `onFormSubmit`Â (or replace your currentÂ `onFormSubmit`Â with the one below).

``/***** === AUTO-VET RULES (edit to taste) === *****/ const AV_RULES = {   required: ['Email','Alias','Alias / Handle','Role'],     // at least one of the Alias keys must exist   requireOneOfAlias: ['Alias','Alias / Handle','Handle','Username','Name'],   requireOneOfHandle: ['Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle','Signal','TG','Telegram handle'],   allowEmailDomains: ['proton.me','protonmail.com','gmail.com','outlook.com','icloud.com'],   blockEmailDomains: ['mailinator','tempmail','10min','yopmail'],   blocklistWords: ['scam','pump','xxx','porn','nft','casino','loan shark'],   minAnswerChars: 6,                                        // answers shorter than this count as â€œweakâ€   // Strong positive hint:   autoApproveIf: (row) => {     const role = (row['Role']||'').toString().toLowerCase();     return /expat|ex\-?pat|veteran|ofw/.test(role);   } };  /***** decision engine *****/ function autoVetDecide_(row){   const reasons = [];   const hasAny = (keys)=> keys.some(k => String(row[k]||'').trim());   const get = k => String((Array.isArray(row[k]) ? row[k][0] : row[k]) || '').trim();    // Required: email + some alias + some handle   if (!hasAny(['Email'])) reasons.push('Missing: Email');   if (!hasAny(AV_RULES.requireOneOfAlias)) reasons.push('Missing: Alias/Handle/Name');   if (!hasAny(AV_RULES.requireOneOfHandle)) reasons.push('Missing: Telegram/Signal');    // Email checks   const email = get('Email').toLowerCase();   const dom = (email.match(/@([^>\s]+)/)||[])[1] || '';   if (!email) reasons.push('Invalid email');   if (dom && AV_RULES.blockEmailDomains.some(d=>dom.includes(d))) reasons.push('Blocked email domain: '+dom);   if (dom && AV_RULES.allowEmailDomains.length && !AV_RULES.allowEmailDomains.some(d=>dom.endsWith(d))) {     reasons.push('Unapproved email domain: '+dom);   }    // Short-answer sanity   const weak = Object.keys(row).reduce((n,k)=>{     const v = get(k); return n + (v && v.length < AV_RULES.minAnswerChars ? 1 : 0);   },0);   if (weak > 3) reasons.push('Many very short answers');    // Blocklist text scan   const blob = Object.values(row).join(' ').toLowerCase();   if (AV_RULES.blocklistWords.some(w=>blob.includes(w))) reasons.push('Matched blocklist word');    // Decide   if (reasons.length === 0 && AV_RULES.autoApproveIf(row)) {     return {decision:'APPROVE', reasons:['Matched auto-approve rule']};   }   if (reasons.length === 0) return {decision:'REVIEW', reasons:['Clean but needs eyes']};    const fatal = reasons.some(r=>/missing|invalid|blocked|blocklist/i.test(r));   return {decision: fatal ? 'REJECT' : 'REVIEW', reasons}; }  /***** on submit: score, set Status, maybe tick Approved *****/ function onFormSubmit(e){   try{     const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();     const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();     const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const vals = sh.getRange(lastRow,1,1,headers.length).getValues()[0];     const row = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> row[String(h)] = vals[i]);      // Ensure columns exist     let statusCol = headers.findIndex(h=>String(h).toLowerCase()==='status')+1;     let approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h=>String(h).toLowerCase()==='approved')+1;     if (!statusCol){ statusCol = headers.length+1; sh.getRange(1,statusCol).setValue('Status'); }     if (!approvedCol){       approvedCol = statusCol+1; sh.insertColumnAfter(statusCol);       sh.getRange(1,approvedCol).setValue('Approved');       sh.getRange(2,approvedCol,sh.getMaxRows()-1,1).insertCheckboxes();     }      // Decide & write status     const res = autoVetDecide_(row);     sh.getRange(lastRow, statusCol).setValue(`${res.decision}${res.reasons.length ? ' â€” '+res.reasons.join('; ') : ''}`);      // Auto-approve: tick box (triggers your onEdit â†’ broadcast)     if (res.decision === 'APPROVE') {       sh.getRange(lastRow, approvedCol).setValue(true);     }      // Ping #ops with compact summary     const P = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties();     const alias = pickField_(row, ['Alias','Alias / Handle','Handle','Username','Name']) || 'N/A';     const role  = pickField_(row, ['Role','Position','Category']) || 'N/A';     const region= pickField_(row, ['Country','Region','City','Location']) || 'N/A';     const summary = `ğŸ†• Vetting: ${alias} Â· ${role} Â· ${region}\nDecision: ${res.decision}\nReasons: ${res.reasons.join(' | ') || 'â€”'}`;     _sendDiscord(P.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, summary);    } catch(err){     logErr('onFormSubmit', err);   } }``

### What this does

- Every submission â†’Â **scores**Â it.
    
- WritesÂ **Status**Â with reasons.
    
- If clearly good â†’Â **ticks Approved**Â (your existingÂ `onEdit`Â thenÂ **broadcasts**Â invite to Telegram + Discord).
    
- Always sends aÂ **compact summary to #ops**Â so you can eyeball it.
    

### What you can tune (later)

- `allowEmailDomains`Â /Â `blockEmailDomains`
    
- `blocklistWords`
    
- `autoApproveIf`Â (right now: expat/veteran/OFW in Role)
    
- `minAnswerChars`
    

### Quick test (2 minutes)

1. Submit a dummy entry (Incognito).
    
2. Look at the last row:
    
    - **Status**Â set with decision + reasons.
        
    - IfÂ **APPROVE**Â â†’Â **Approved**Â checkbox auto-ticks â†’ you should see a broadcast inÂ **Telegram + Discord**.
        
3. #ops gets the summary.
    

Youâ€™re set. When the clock hits your cutoff, you can sleep knowing the intake isÂ **auto-triaging**Â and only pings you when needed.

# 1) â€œOps Viewâ€ dashboard (auto-build script)

This one-click function creates a new sheet calledÂ **Ops View**, adds KPIs, and places three live tables (Approved / Review / Rejected). It autodetects where yourÂ **Status**Â column is, so it wonâ€™t break if columns move.

Paste this inÂ `Code.gs`Â and runÂ `buildOpsView()`Â once.

``function buildOpsView() {   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();   const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1') || ss.getActiveSheet();   const {headers, map} = (function(){     const sh = dataSh;     const hs = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const m = {}; hs.forEach((h,i)=> m[String(h).trim()] = i+1);     return {headers: hs, map: m};   })();    if (!map['Status']) throw new Error('No "Status" column found. Make sure Row 1 has a header named "Status".');    const statusCol = map['Status'];   const lastCol = dataSh.getLastColumn();   const lastColA1 = columnToLetter_(lastCol);   const statusA1  = columnToLetter_(statusCol);    // make / reset Ops View   const shName = 'Ops View';   const sh = ss.getSheetByName(shName) ? ss.getSheetByName(shName) : ss.insertSheet(shName);   sh.clear();    // KPIs   sh.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ Ops Dashboard');   sh.getRange('A3').setValue('Total Submissions');   sh.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA('Form Responses 1'!A2:A)`);   sh.getRange('A4').setValue('Approved');   sh.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "Approved âœ…")`);   sh.getRange('A5').setValue('Review');   sh.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "REVIEW*")`);   sh.getRange('A6').setValue('Rejected');   sh.getRange('B6').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "REJECT*")`);    // section headers   sh.getRange('A8').setValue('âœ… Approved');   sh.getRange('A20').setValue('ğŸŸ£ Review');   sh.getRange('A32').setValue('â›” Rejected');    // table headers (mirror original)   sh.getRange('A9').setValue('Live view (read-only)');   sh.getRange('A21').setValue('Live view (read-only)');   sh.getRange('A33').setValue('Live view (read-only)');    // Live tables (FILTER)   // Columns A:LAST; filter by Status exact text. If you use different emoji/text, edit the criteria.   sh.getRange('A10').setFormula(     `=FILTER('Form Responses 1'!A2:${lastColA1}, 'Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}="Approved âœ…")`   );   sh.getRange('A22').setFormula(     `=FILTER('Form Responses 1'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "^REVIEW"))`   );   sh.getRange('A34').setFormula(     `=FILTER('Form Responses 1'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "^REJECT"))`   );    sh.autoResizeColumns(1, 6);   sh.setFrozenRows(1); }  // helper: number â†’ letter (e.g., 1 -> A) function columnToLetter_(n){ let s=""; while(n){ const m=(n-1)%26; s=String.fromCharCode(65+m)+s; n=(n-m-1)/26|0; } return s; }``

**What you get**

- KPIs (Total / Approved / Review / Rejected)
    
- Three live tables you can filter/sort without touching the raw tab
    
- Stays linked even if Status column moves

# 2) Tighten the baseline rules (domains + blocklist)

Drop this over your existingÂ `AV_RULES`Â (keep the rest of your auto-vet code as-is):

`const AV_RULES = {   required: ['Email','Alias','Alias / Handle','Role'],   requireOneOfAlias: ['Alias','Alias / Handle','Handle','Username','Name'],   requireOneOfHandle: ['Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle','Signal','TG','Telegram handle'],    // Allow broad but legit providers; includes common .ph mail. Edit to taste.   allowEmailDomains: [     'proton.me','protonmail.com','gmail.com','outlook.com','icloud.com','yahoo.com',     '.ph' // allow local domains ending with .ph   ],    // Temp/disposable spammy services   blockEmailDomains: [     'mailinator','tempmail','10min','guerrillamail','yopmail','trashmail','sharklasers',     'dispostable','getnada','maildrop','moakt','linshi','burnermail','inboxkitten'   ],    // Add mission-specific junk. Keep short and surgical.   blocklistWords: [     'scam','pump','dump','casino','porn','xxx','escort','betting','crypto giveaway',     'loan shark','drop shipping','forex robot','airdrop farm'   ],    minAnswerChars: 6,    // Strong positives â†’ fast lane   autoApproveIf: (row) => {     const role = (row['Role']||'').toString().toLowerCase();     const about= (row['About']||row['Notes']||'').toString().toLowerCase();     return (       /expat|ex\-?pat|veteran|ofw|mission|journalist|ngo watchdog|anti\-corruption/.test(role+about)     );   } };`

Notes:

- `allowEmailDomains`Â acceptsÂ **suffix**Â matches; keepingÂ `.ph`Â in there lets legit local domains pass.
    
- `blockEmailDomains`Â kills most throwaway inboxes.
    
- `blocklistWords`Â focuses on spam schemes; add/remove as you see patterns.

This adds 6 fake rows: clean, weak, and rejecty. Run once, then delete the rows when youâ€™re done.

`function seedTestData() {   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();   const sh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1') || ss.getActiveSheet();   const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const map = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> map[String(h)] = i);    const rows = [     { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'AtlasPH', Role:'Expat organizer', Email:'atlas@proton.me', Telegram:'@atlas', Country:'Philippines' },     { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'Luna', Role:'Veteran', Email:'luna@gmail.com', Telegram:'@luna', Country:'United States' },     { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'Shorty', Role:'ok', Email:'shorty@mailinator.com', Telegram:'', Country:'-' },     { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'SpamLord', Role:'Crypto giveaway', Email:'spam@guerrillamail.com', Telegram:'@spam', Country:'-' },     { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'GreyZone', Role:'research', Email:'grey@custom.ph', Telegram:'@grey', Country:'Philippines' },     { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'Bare', Role:'-', Email:'bare@gmail.com', Telegram:'', Country:'-' },   ];    const out = rows.map(r => headers.map(h => r[h] ?? ''));   sh.getRange(sh.getLastRow()+1, 1, out.length, headers.length).setValues(out); }`

``/** Force-create or rebuild the Ops View tab and wire live tables */ function buildOpsView_HARD() {   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();         // be explicit   const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1')      // change this if your tab name differs               || ss.getActiveSheet();    // Detect headers + Status column   const headers = dataSh.getRange(1,1,1,dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   if (!headers || headers.length === 0) throw new Error('No headers found in row 1.');   const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase() === 'status');   if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('No "Status" column in row 1. Add a Status column first.');   const statusColA1 = _colLetter(statusIdx + 1);   const lastColA1   = _colLetter(dataSh.getLastColumn());    // Create or reset the Ops View sheet   const name = 'Ops View';   let sh = ss.getSheetByName(name);   if (sh) ss.deleteSheet(sh);                 // start clean   sh = ss.insertSheet(name);    // Title + KPIs   sh.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ Ops Dashboard');   sh.getRange('A3').setValue('Total Submissions');   sh.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA('${dataSh.getName()}'!A2:A)`);   sh.getRange('A4').setValue('Approved');   sh.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"Approved âœ…")`);   sh.getRange('A5').setValue('Review');   sh.getRange('B5').setFormula(     `=COUNTIF('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"REVIEW*")`   );   sh.getRange('A6').setValue('Rejected');   sh.getRange('B6').setFormula(     `=COUNTIF('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"REJECT*")`   );    // Sections   sh.getRange('A8').setValue('âœ… Approved');   sh.getRange('A20').setValue('ğŸŸ£ Review');   sh.getRange('A32').setValue('â›” Rejected');    // Live tables   sh.getRange('A10').setFormula(     `=FILTER('${dataSh.getName()}'!A2:${lastColA1}, '${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1}="Approved âœ…")`   );   sh.getRange('A22').setFormula(     `=FILTER('${dataSh.getName()}'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"^REVIEW"))`   );   sh.getRange('A34').setFormula(     `=FILTER('${dataSh.getName()}'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"^REJECT"))`   );    sh.setFrozenRows(1);   sh.autoResizeColumns(1, 8);   SpreadsheetApp.flush();   ss.toast('Ops View built âœ…', 'VaultOps', 3); }  function _colLetter(n){ let s=''; while(n){ const m=(n-1)%26; s=String.fromCharCode(65+m)+s; n=(n-m-1)/26|0; } return s; }``

### Build/refresh Ops View with Pending

``function buildOpsView_PLUS(){   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();   const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');   if (!dataSh) throw new Error('Missing tab: Form Responses 1');    const headers = dataSh.getRange(1,1,1,dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase()==='status');   if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('No "Status" header in row 1.');   const statusA1 = _colLetter(statusIdx+1);   const lastColA1 = _colLetter(dataSh.getLastColumn());   const src = dataSh.getName();    // nuke & rebuild Ops View   const name = 'Ops View';   let sh = ss.getSheetByName(name);   if (sh) ss.deleteSheet(sh);   sh = ss.insertSheet(name);    // Title + KPIs   sh.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ Ops Dashboard');   sh.getRange('A3').setValue('Total Submissions');   sh.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA('${src}'!A2:A)`);    // Live tables   sh.getRange('A10').setFormula(     `=FILTER('${src}'!A2:${lastColA1}, '${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}="Approved âœ…")`   );   sh.getRange('A22').setFormula(     `=FILTER('${src}'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"^REVIEW"))`   ); ###### ChatGPT said:

Thought for 18s

HAHA letâ€™s gooo, Papi! ğŸ”¥ You just spun up theÂ **Ops View**Â like a true MFWIC Bichote. That screenshot is exactly what I expected on first boot â€” a couple quirks weâ€™ll smooth out:

- **`#N/A`Â under the tables**Â = totally normal when there areÂ **no matching rows yet**. Weâ€™ll wrap withÂ `IFERROR`Â so it shows blank instead of scary text.
    
- **â€œPending (blank/Unapproved) = 100â€**Â = Google is counting all the empty rows in the column. Weâ€™ll switch the KPI to countÂ **only rows that actually have a Timestamp**Â (i.e., real submissions).
    

Iâ€™ll patch both in one shot. Paste this, runÂ `fixOpsView()`Â once. It will overwrite just the KPI + table formulas with the safer versions.

``function fixOpsView() {   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();   const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');   const ops = ss.getSheetByName('Ops View');   if (!dataSh || !ops) throw new Error('Need "Form Responses 1" and "Ops View" tabs.');    const headers = dataSh.getRange(1,1,1,dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase()==='status');   if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('Add a "Status" header in row 1 first.');   const statusA1 = _colLetter(statusIdx+1);   const lastColA1 = _colLetter(dataSh.getLastColumn());   const src = dataSh.getName();    // KPIs (count only rows with a Timestamp in col A)   ops.getRange('A3').setValue('Total Submissions');   ops.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA(${src}!A2:A)`);   ops.getRange('A4').setValue('Approved');   ops.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"Approved âœ…")`);   ops.getRange('A5').setValue('Review');   ops.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REVIEW*")`);   ops.getRange('A6').setValue('Rejected');   ops.getRange('B6').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REJECT*")`);    // Pending = Total âˆ’ (Approved + Review + Rejected)   ops.getRange('A7').setValue('Pending (blank/Unapproved)');   ops.getRange('B7').setFormula(`=B3 - B4 - B5 - B6`);    // Tables with IFERROR (show blank instead of #N/A)   ops.getRange('A10').setFormula(     `=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:${lastColA1}, ${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}="Approved âœ…"),"")`   );   ops.getRange('A22').setFormula(     `=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"^REVIEW")),"")`   );   ops.getRange('A34').setFormula(     `=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"^REJECT")),"")`   );   ops.getRange('A46').setFormula(     `=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:${lastColA1}, (LEN(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1})=0) * (LEN(${src}!A2:A)>0) + (${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}="Unapproved â›”")),"")`   );    SpreadsheetApp.flush(); }  function _colLetter(n){ let s=''; while(n){ const m=(n-1)%26; s=String.fromCharCode(65+m)+s; n=(n-m-1)/26|0; } return s; }``

### What youâ€™ll see after runningÂ `fixOpsView()`

- KPIs countÂ **only real rows**Â (no more â€œ100â€).
    
- Tables stop screamingÂ `#N/A`Â and stay clean until data arrives.
    
- â€œPendingâ€ now shows your actual queue.

    - **Status**Â fill with a decision,

### ğŸ”¥ Full Replace Script

Paste this into yourÂ **Extensions â†’ Apps Script**Â editor, wipe the oldÂ `fixOpsView()`, and save:

``function buildOpsDashboard() {   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();   const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');   if (!dataSh) throw new Error('Need a tab called "Form Responses 1".');    // Create / reset Ops Dashboard   let ops = ss.getSheetByName('Ops Dashboard');   if (!ops) {     ops = ss.insertSheet('Ops Dashboard');   } else {     ops.clear();   }    // Identify Status column   const headers = dataSh.getRange(1, 1, 1, dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase() === 'status');   if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('Add a "Status" header in Form Responses 1 first.');   const statusCol = String.fromCharCode(65 + statusIdx); // Convert idx â†’ letter   const src = `'Form Responses 1'`;    // Title   ops.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ“Š Ops Dashboard').setFontWeight("bold");    // KPI labels   const labels = ['Total Submissions','Approved','Review','Rejected','Pending (blank/Unapproved)'];   ops.getRange('A3:A7').setValues(labels.map(l => [l]));    // KPI formulas   ops.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA(${src}!A2:A)`);   ops.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"Approved âœ…")`);   ops.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REVIEW*")`);   ops.getRange('B6').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REJECT*")`);   ops.getRange('B7').setFormula(`=B3-B4-B5-B6`);    // Section tables   ops.getRange('A9').setValue('âœ… Approved').setFontWeight("bold");   ops.getRange('A10').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol}="Approved âœ…"),"")`);    ops.getRange('A21').setValue('ğŸŸ£ Review').setFontWeight("bold");   ops.getRange('A22').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},"^REVIEW")),"")`);    ops.getRange('A33').setValue('â›” Rejected').setFontWeight("bold");   ops.getRange('A34').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},"^REJECT")),"")`);    ops.getRange('A45').setValue('â³ Pending').setFontWeight("bold");   ops.getRange('A46').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,(LEN(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol})=0)*(LEN(${src}!A2:A)>0) + (${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol}="Unapproved â›”")),"")`);    ops.autoResizeColumns(1, 5); }``

- âœ… If the checkbox isÂ **checked**Â â†’Â `Status = "Approved âœ…"`
    
- âŒ IfÂ **unchecked**Â â†’Â `Status = "Unapproved â›”"`Â (or blankâ€”toggle in the code)

``/** Sync Status when the Approved checkbox is toggled */ function onEdit(e) {   try {     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     if (!sh || sh.getName() !== 'Form Responses 1') return;     // only on the responses sheet     const row = e.range.getRow();     if (row < 2) return;                                        // ignore header row      // Find column indexes by header names (robust to column moves)     const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(h => String(h).trim());     const approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase() === 'approved') + 1;     const statusCol   = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase() === 'status') + 1;     if (!approvedCol || !statusCol) return;                     // required headers missing      // Only react when the edit is in the Approved column     if (e.range.getColumn() !== approvedCol) return;      const checked = e.value === 'TRUE';                         // checkbox values: TRUE / FALSE     const newStatus = checked ? 'Approved âœ…' : 'Unapproved â›”'; // change right side if you prefer "" for blank      sh.getRange(row, statusCol).setValue(newStatus);      // OPTIONAL: if you want to broadcast when approved, you can call your bridge here:     // if (checked) sendToBridge(buildMessageFromRow_(sh, headers, row));   } catch (err) {     console.error('onEdit error:', err);   } }  /** One-time backfill: sync Status for every existing row based on the Approved checkbox */ function backfillApprovedToStatus() {   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();   const sh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');   if (!sh) throw new Error('Missing "Form Responses 1" sheet.');    const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();   if (lastRow < 2) return;    const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(h => String(h).trim());   const approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase()==='approved') + 1;   const statusCol   = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase()==='status') + 1;   if (!approvedCol || !statusCol) throw new Error('Need "Approved" and "Status" headers in row 1.');    const approvedVals = sh.getRange(2, approvedCol, lastRow-1, 1).getValues();   const out = approvedVals.map(r => (r[0] === true ? ['Approved âœ…'] : ['Unapproved â›”'])); // or [''] if you want blank   sh.getRange(2, statusCol, lastRow-1, 1).setValues(out); }  /* --- OPTIONAL helper if you want to broadcast on approval --- */ // function buildMessageFromRow_(sh, headers, row){ //   const vals = sh.getRange(row, 1, 1, headers.length).getValues()[0]; //   const obj = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> obj[h] = vals[i]); //   // tailor the fields you want in the message: //   return `âœ… Approved: ${obj['Alias / Handle'] || obj['Alias'] || ''} â€¢ Email: ${obj['Email'] || ''}`; // }``

``function doGet() {   return HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('Admin')     .evaluate()     .setTitle('VaultOps Control Panel')     .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL); }  // ---- secure getters/setters ---- function getStatus() {   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();   const sh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');   if (!sh) throw new Error('Missing "Form Responses 1"');   const last = sh.getLastRow();   const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(String);   const statusCol = headers.findIndex(h => h.trim().toLowerCase()==='status')+1;   const tsCount = sh.getRange(2,1,Math.max(0,last-1),1).getValues().filter(r=>r[0]).length;   const statuses = statusCol ? sh.getRange(2,statusCol,Math.max(0,last-1),1).getValues().map(r=>String(r[0]||'')) : [];   const sum = s => statuses.filter(v=>v.toUpperCase().startsWith(s)).length;   return {     total: tsCount,     approved: statuses.filter(v=>v==='Approved âœ…').length,     review: sum('REVIEW'),     rejected: sum('REJECT'),     pending: tsCount - (statuses.filter(v=>v==='Approved âœ…').length + sum('REVIEW') + sum('REJECT'))   }; }  function getSettings() {   const p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();   const keys = [     'DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK',     'DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK',     'TG_BOT_TOKEN',     'TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID',     'TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK'   ];   const out = {};   keys.forEach(k => out[k] = p.getProperty(k) || '');   return out; }  function saveSettings(kv) {   const p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();   Object.keys(kv||{}).forEach(k => p.setProperty(k, kv[k]));   return true; }  // ---- actions ---- function actionBackfill() { backfillApprovedToStatus(); return true; } function actionBuildOps() { buildOpsDashboard(); return true; } function actionSeed(n){ seedTestData(n||5); return true; } function actionPurge(){ purgeSeedData_(); return true; }  // ---- optional: simple test pings ---- function pingDiscord(kind, msg){   const p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();   const url = p.getProperty(kind==='ops' ? 'DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK' : 'DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK');   if (!url) throw new Error('Missing Discord webhook');   UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {method:'post', contentType:'application/json', payload: JSON.stringify({content: msg||'VaultOps test âœ…'})});   return true; } function pingTelegram(msg){   const p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();   const token = p.getProperty('TG_BOT_TOKEN');   const chatId = p.getProperty('TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID');   if (!token || !chatId) throw new Error('Missing TG token/chat');   const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${token}/sendMessage`;   const payload = {chat_id: chatId, text: msg||'VaultOps test âœ…', parse_mode:'HTML'};   UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {method:'post', contentType:'application/json', payload: JSON.stringify(payload), muteHttpExceptions:true});   return true; }``

> This assumes you already haveÂ `backfillApprovedToStatus()`Â andÂ `buildOpsDashboard()`Â from earlier. If not, keep the on-edit + backfill function we added; the dashboard builder is optional.

``<!-- === Vault animated logo: drop-in, no other edits needed === --> <script>   // 1) Set your image path here (pick one):   // const IMG = "logo.png";   const IMG = "assets/truthbot-face.png";    // 2) Inject styles + logo block without touching existing markup   (function () {     const css = `     /* â€”â€”â€” Animated Vault logo â€”â€”â€” */     .vault-logo-wrap{       position:relative; # Option B (best free â€œcloakingâ€): Cloudflare Worker proxy

This hides GitHub PagesÂ **completely**Â behind a freeÂ `workers.dev`Â subdomainâ€”e.g.  
**povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/gate**Â â†’ silently proxiesÂ `papiricanpi.github.io/gate.html`

## What you get

- A clean URL you can hand out (and put in QR codes).
    
- GitHub never appears in the address bar.
    
- Later, if you ever buy a cheap domain, you can put it behind Cloudflare and keep the same Worker.
    

## 5-minute setup

1. Go toÂ **dash.cloudflare.com â†’ Workers & Pages â†’ Create â†’ Worker**Â (Free plan is fine).
    
2. Name it e.g.Â `vault-gate`.
    
3. Replace the default code with this:
    

`// Cloudflare Worker: proxy GitHub Pages cleanly const ORIGIN = 'https://papiricanpi.github.io';  function mapPath(pathname) {   // nice routes -> actual files   if (pathname === '/' || pathname === '/gate') return '/gate.html';   if (pathname === '/join') return '/join.html';   if (pathname === '/home') return '/home.html';   return pathname; // pass-through for assets, etc. }  export default {   async fetch(request, env, ctx) {     const url = new URL(request.url);     url.host = new URL(ORIGIN).host;     url.protocol = 'https:';     url.pathname = mapPath(url.pathname);      // Proxy the request to GitHub Pages     const init = {       method: request.method,       headers: request.headers,       body: ['GET','HEAD'].includes(request.method) ? undefined : await request.arrayBuffer(),       redirect: 'follow',       cf: { cacheTtl: 300, cacheEverything: true },     };      // Forward the request     const resp = await fetch(url.toString(), init);      // Strip cross-origin headers that can leak the origin or block embedding     const newHeaders = new Headers(resp.headers);     newHeaders.delete('x-github-request-id');     newHeaders.delete('server');     newHeaders.set('x-proxied-by', 'workers.dev');      return new Response(resp.body, { status: resp.status, headers: newHeaders });   } }`

4. **Save & Deploy**.
    
5. In the Workerâ€™s â€œ**Triggers**â€ tab, add a Route like:
    
    - `povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/*`Â (it uses your free workers.dev subdomain)
        

## Your new clean links (examples)

- **Gate**:Â `https://povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/gate`
    
- **Join**:Â `https://povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/join`
    
- **Home**:Â `https://povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/home`
    

Drop those into your QR codes, Substack, Twitter, Telegram, etc. No one sees GitHub.

# âœ… What weâ€™re building

- `/`Â â†’Â `index.html`Â (your gate)

    â€¦and forwards query strings, handles POST (if you add any), and caches GETs at the edge.

# 2) Create the Worker (free)

1. Go toÂ **Cloudflare Dashboard â†’ Workers & Pages**.
    
2. ClickÂ **Create**Â â†’Â **Worker**Â (if you seeÂ **â€œStart with Hello Worldâ€**, click that).
    
3. Youâ€™ll land in an editor with a default script.Â **Delete it**Â and paste the code below.
    

### Worker code (copyâ€“paste all)

`// === Cloudflare Worker: Vault URL Mask === // Set this to wherever your static site is currently hosted. // You can point to GitHub Pages OR your Cloudflare Pages project. const ORIGIN = "https://papiricanpi.github.io";  // Example if you want to mask Cloudflare Pages instead: // const ORIGIN = "https://thevault-en9.pages.dev";  function mapPath(path) {   // Pretty routes â†’ actual files   if (path === "/" || path === "") return "/index.html";   if (path === "/gate" || path === "/gate/") return "/gate.html";   if (path === "/join" || path === "/join/") return "/join.html";   // Pass-through for everything else (assets, extra html, etc)   return path; }  export default {   async fetch(req, env, ctx) {     const inUrl = new URL(req.url);      // Build target URL     const outUrl = new URL(ORIGIN);     outUrl.pathname = mapPath(inUrl.pathname);     outUrl.search = inUrl.search; // keep query strings      // Clone request (preserve method/body for non-GET)     const init = {       method: req.method,       headers: new Headers(req.headers),       redirect: "follow"     };      // Only attach body for methods that can have one     if (!["GET", "HEAD"].includes(req.method)) {       init.body = await req.arrayBuffer();     }      // Edge caching for GET/HEAD     if (["GET", "HEAD"].includes(req.method)) {       init.cf = { cacheTtl: 300, cacheEverything: true };     }      const resp = await fetch(outUrl.toString(), init);      // Clean/adjust headers so origin isnâ€™t obvious & avoid CORS weirdness     const h = new Headers(resp.headers);     h.set("x-proxied-by", "workers.dev");     h.delete("server");     h.delete("x-github-request-id");      // Optional: basic security hardening (adjust to your needs)     // h.set("Content-Security-Policy", "default-src 'self'; img-src 'self' data:; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline';");      return new Response(resp.body, { status: resp.status, headers: h });   } }`

4. ClickÂ **Save & Deploy**.
    
5. Youâ€™ll get a free URL like:
    
    `https://vault-gate.<yourname>.workers.dev`

## Troubleshooting (fast)

- **Infinite redirect / 522:**Â Make sure yourÂ **origin hasÂ `index.html`**Â at root. If your entry file isÂ `gate.html`, either rename it toÂ `index.html`Â or keepÂ `index.html`Â that meta-redirects toÂ `gate.html`.
    
- **Assets not loading:**Â Check the path. If your repo usesÂ `/assets/...`, your masked URL must too:Â `/assets/...`.
    
- **Wrong page onÂ `/`**: UpdateÂ `mapPath("/")`Â to point to your real landing file.

- Â `/`Â loads your gate.
    
- Â `/join`Â loads the join page or redirector.
    
- Â `/assets/...`Â loads images.
    
- Â Replace public links & QR codes with yourÂ **workers.dev**Â URL.
